<username>Robert<//username><Time>1547319192919</Time><rating>5</rating>< Text>
This bar looks a bit rough from the outside, but let me tell you - venture inside and you're in for a treat. There isn't a lot to offer in terms of bar games, but the atmosphere is fantastic. Not to mention the bartenders who are quick, attentive, and know their stuff.

They have karaoke nights and the karaoke here is unlike anywhere else. Usually the music switches between country and rap with no rhyme or reason as to when the switch will happen or why. You'll have 60 year-olds singing rap, and then a 20-something go up and sing country. Regardless of what's being sung or who's doing it though, the entire bar gets extremely into it.

This is definitely an older crowd than typically goes to places like Lucky Lukes, but just as fun if not moreso.<//Text>

L and L =Love and Love this place

Im a regular here.  The food is great, economical and easy.

Its mostly a take out place but they do have chairs for people who want to eat there.   Its not really a sit down restaurant where someone takes your order, you order from the cashier and they call you when your food is ready.

Parking is easy, top level and below ground free parking.  If you are picking up, call ahead.

They also have a rewards program, tenth meal is free.

Im not comparing it to a five star restaurant but for the money, its really great Hawaiian style  fast food

Chicken Teriyaki - Really good
Spam Musubi - Really good
Chicken Katu- really good
Fried fish - really good
Macaroni salad good

Fries- meh

They also have a selection of beer and hawaiian drinks.

The staff is friendly (pretty much the same girl or two).  And she needs a raise, she is a hard worker and ALWAYS friendly.  I saw her at Starbucks once and bought her a coffee.

Ive met the owner a couple of times, very humble, nice Japanese guy who takes pride in his store.

This place is really great, cant say enough about it, has become one of my go to weeknight meals.< /Text>

< text>
Went to the 2nd level store today and was met by a very rude, miserable woman.
I understand people may be having a bad day, that's fine but this was beyond that. Per CoVid only 4 people are allowed in the store at once. Myself and family made 3 so we were the only ones in there. The employee had just finished up with someone, figuring she would help us after or at least greet us (I had enough time to pick out what I wanted as she helped the previous customer) we waited... And waited... And waited. Until finally after ten mins my family member asks if we can get some help. Without looking up from her computer and, "what do you need?" My sister points at the hat and describes the hat, still the employee doesn't look up, walks to the wall of hats and asks again which hat we want to see. She hands it to us without any type of customer service, how is it going out further assistance and walks away. I had some questions to which she rudely and condescendingly replied to. I returned the hat and walked out. Do yourself a favor and go to the Lids downstairs, hopefully she doesn't work there.</text>

< review>
Just recently started playing golf about a month ago. Got some used clubs and have been learning about the game. I came into this store for the first time because one of my clubs was too long for me. I found out that you can cut down and even add length to your irons. So I came here to get my iron cut down. It was 2.5 inches over standard size from what the tech told me. He cut it down the shaft to standard length for me and was even able save and reused my grip.  As of 7/92020. It was $3.99 to cut down the shaft & $5.99 to salvage and re-grip the club. < review>
Sales manager Steve was a great help. He called to me when I was looking at a driver. Gave me many insights into drivers, and even suggested an older model as being very good but way marked down. Steve wasn't the only employee to help me as I spent about an hour trying out various drivers at their nice practice net facilty. The screen you hit in has a graphic representation of what your shot would look like. I was looking for a new driver. Drivers being expensive, Steve suggested I try a few, come back more than once and keep trying until I was confident. He also mentioned an older model similar to one I was trying, which was steeply discounted. I really felt they were trying to help me get the best club for my use and budget. As far as golf equipment, I'll come back here for it.< /review>

<rate>1< /rate>< Review>
About two years ago I went to Golfsmith in San Jose to get fitted and replace shafts of my 3 and 4 irons. The order was to install +1/2" longer than standard DG S300s. The result? 3i was 39.5" (looks good but it's not over) and 4i was standard 38.5". Drove in again to get 4i extended to 38.75" since I thought +1/4" would be OK. Then I found the grip on 3i was not firmly installed, so it was actually 39.25". Alright I had to replace the grip.

That's not the end of the story. Today I just found that the 3i was actually soft stepped and 4i was double soft stepped...?! My god! After all these years! No wonder I've always felt weird when playing 3i/4i/5i together!

I had much better experience going to Golfmart in Dublin area. They may have a smaller shop but service is IMPECCABLE.< /Review>

<rating>5<//rating>< review>
I'm not one to write business reviews but I had such a positive experience here that I feel compelled to share my experience.  My wife and I have passed by this place for many years but have never had the need for extra storage space.  Without going into details, we recently had a family member that needed a lot of household items put into a storage facility. We debated about whether to give up our own garage space or consider renting a storage facility.  Our own garage would be an easy choice but it also meant giving up our space -- which we weren't too fond of (especially my wife.)  We decided to check out Extra Space Storage on Main St. and I couldn't be happier that we did.  We had no idea how it worked or what our options were.  We met with a woman (I think her name was Roberta?) that was incredibly helpful and supportive, particularly given we had no idea what we were doing and the family situation we were dealing with.  She really helped us get a better grasp on what our storage size needs might be as well as providing us detailed information about security, access, etc.  We were so impressed that we didn't even look at other facilities and have moved all the items into storage.  We've been back several times and always have great interactions with the staff. In fact, I think we may consider renting another space for some unused items we currently have in our home but aren't quite ready to part with. I'm just really impressed with this facility and our interaction with the staff.< /review>

< review>
The people at Extra Space Storage were very helpful and friendly.  I had reserved a unit on-line.  When I got there the gentleman took us around to the unit which was reserved for us and asked if the size was ok.  I told him we would need a bigger unit.  He took us to see the next largest unit.  There was no problem in changing my request.  The location was perfect and the facility was very clean.  Being able to give them just a few days notice prior to vacating was great.  Most facilities require a 30-day notice.  If I have to store items again I would definitely go there first and if I know of anyone needing storage, I would definitely recommend Extra Space Storage.</review>
